msg:I booked this hotel for one night as I had a long layover in Shenzhen and needed to be at the airport the next afternoon. The hotel is located near the Shekou Ferry port (transfer to HK Airport and so on). It is very close to the Seaworld subway station, exit E is just 50 meters from the entrance. The staff was extremely friendly and welcoming even at late check in. I especially want to thank ÊôìÊô¥ for the best service. 
The room was extremely beautiful, modern, well equipped. Comfortable bed, big bathroom and a huge shower. All necessary items were provided, in addition to FREE minibar drinks. The breakfast choices offer a decent variety and are satisfying. Even though it understandably doesnt offer much western food choices. Check out was quick and easy and the subway ride from the hotel to the airport took like 25 min with only 1 interchange. Overall a solid 5/5 stars

The environment and room hygiene are very clean, which makes people feel very comfortable. Secondly, the hotel has a very good location, convenient transportation, and prosperous surroundings. It is very close to the Sea World and the beach, and it is also convenient to go to Shekou Port. The hotel price is also very reasonable. Compared with the rooms of the same price hotels in the surrounding areas, Jiuzhou Hotel has a high cost performance and is worth recommending. During the stay, the hotel lobby housekeeper Lili provided very good service and deserves praise. I will choose Jiuzhou next time I come.

posted:Posted May 12, 2023
msg:If you are a tourist arriving in Shenzhen via public transportation, this hotel is undoubtedly in an excellent location. You are just outside the subway station, business district, and Dananshan Park. It is very convenient for eating, supper, morning exercise, and going to other places in the city

However, if you are going by car, it is recommended to carefully consider choosing this hotel, because there are very few parking spaces. Although there is an underground garage, there are less than 20 available parking spaces, and there are only about 50 parking spaces on the ground. The restaurant in this building is shared with another hotel... It is conceivable that the parking on holidays is a nigh**are level, and the on-site staff are not helpful. They will tell you to park at the Prince's Square opposite, but they charge a fee Ah (capped at 60 yuan for 24 hours), would you like to stay in a hotel and pay for the parking fee yourself?

The overall level of breakfast is near the standard line. There are freshly cooked noodle stalls and fried eggs, but the overall food types are relatively small and the quality is average. The key point is that there are too few seats, and there is a lack of on-site management. A large number of family guests sit for two People then moved the chairs of other tables for their own use, so there were many vacancies with tables but no chairs... In addition, the restaurant piled up kitchen utensils in the emergency evacuation stairwell, which made the stairs completely unable to go up and down normally. What is the nature of this? Please judge for yourself

The room itself is not bad, although the space is not spacious, it has everything you need (the separation of the shower room is a bit wasteful), and the drinks in the minibar and small refrigerator are free

Praise the manager Cai at the front desk for helping to deal with the parking fee reduction and exemption when checking out
